function warn($str) { echo "WARNING: $str\n"; }
function err($str) { die("FATAL ERROR: $str\n"); }

	warn('Directory could not be created: setup/img');

	warn('Could not change directory permissions of setup/img');
}

if (is_file('setup/img/main_icon.png') && (sha1_file('setup/img/main_icon.png') != 'a13c7ab77af05994eaed57ddc907957e5b60cf99')) {
	warn('File was created by someone else. Will overwrite the changes now: setup/img/main_icon.png');
	$tmp = pathinfo('setup/img/main_icon.png');
	$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('setup/img/main_icon.png')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
	warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
	if (!@copy('setup/img/main_icon.png', $backup_name)) {
		warn('Creation of backup failed');
	}
}
writefile_1();
if (!is_file('setup/img/main_icon.png')) {
	warn('File cannot be created (not existing): setup/img/main_icon.png');
} else if (sha1_file('setup/img/main_icon.png') != 'a13c7ab77af05994eaed57ddc907957e5b60cf99') {
	warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): setup/img/main_icon.png');
} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('setup/img/main_icon.png', 0644)) {
	warn('Could not change file permissions of setup/img/main_icon.png');
}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
	writefile_2();
	if (!is_file('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php') != '24d60dc445b43a417e7773889d4802583a0eba6d') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php') !== '24d60dc445b43a417e7773889d4802583a0eba6d') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php') !== '2934474994ff422ca8d43ead7abc1d6a82979af2') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php') !== '24d60dc445b43a417e7773889d4802583a0eba6d') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
		}
	}
}

	writefile_3();
	if (!is_file('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php') != '80e3fafb447c0dc7aafa2f19bc44695bc77ba9fe') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php') !== '80e3fafb447c0dc7aafa2f19bc44695bc77ba9fe') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php') !== 'aefdd4a47c46590bd54d52b1b4f79ec7c021e76e') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_3();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php') !== '80e3fafb447c0dc7aafa2f19bc44695bc77ba9fe') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplusGui.class.php');

	writefile_10();
	if (!is_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') != '864f8183f56ed254f4176899bd145c8cb0fd22fa') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '864f8183f56ed254f4176899bd145c8cb0fd22fa') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== 'b818ea345a8110df45579d12d1ee1744656153bd') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_10();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '864f8183f56ed254f4176899bd145c8cb0fd22fa') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('setup/includes/setup_base.js')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: setup/includes/setup_base.js');
	writefile_13();
	if (!is_file('setup/includes/setup_base.js')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): setup/includes/setup_base.js');
	} else if (sha1_file('setup/includes/setup_base.js') != 'd0a4872652e835ffe78d8e5adb77b0ff578d9a5d') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): setup/includes/setup_base.js');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('setup/includes/setup_base.js', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of setup/includes/setup_base.js');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('setup/includes/setup_base.js') !== 'd0a4872652e835ffe78d8e5adb77b0ff578d9a5d') {
		if (@sha1_file('setup/includes/setup_base.js') !== '781162ec32bcc868b7ad9fa9e26fd38f32c91a13') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: setup/includes/setup_base.js');
			$tmp = pathinfo('setup/includes/setup_base.js');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('setup/includes/setup_base.js')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('setup/includes/setup_base.js', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_13();
		if (@sha1_file('setup/includes/setup_base.js') !== 'd0a4872652e835ffe78d8e5adb77b0ff578d9a5d') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): setup/includes/setup_base.js');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('setup/index.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: setup/index.php');
	writefile_14();
	if (!is_file('setup/index.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): setup/index.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('setup/index.php') != '873bcc8da8abc801e8e3a92325fa213f14aac05f') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): setup/index.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('setup/index.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of setup/index.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('setup/index.php') !== '873bcc8da8abc801e8e3a92325fa213f14aac05f') {
		if (@sha1_file('setup/index.php') !== '5de391898d8c85051349ef216bc3b0f40b113b43') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: setup/index.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('setup/index.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('setup/index.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('setup/index.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_14();
		if (@sha1_file('setup/index.php') !== '873bcc8da8abc801e8e3a92325fa213f14aac05f') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): setup/index.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('setup/setup.min.js.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: setup/setup.min.js.php');
	writefile_15();
	if (!is_file('setup/setup.min.js.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): setup/setup.min.js.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('setup/setup.min.js.php') != '451dd1d330eafccd631e27b18ed4667ce3f9be77') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): setup/setup.min.js.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('setup/setup.min.js.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of setup/setup.min.js.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('setup/setup.min.js.php') !== '451dd1d330eafccd631e27b18ed4667ce3f9be77') {
		if (@sha1_file('setup/setup.min.js.php') !== '17069781b7b0cf823f770532c0c6039a41eb9386') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: setup/setup.min.js.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('setup/setup.min.js.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('setup/setup.min.js.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('setup/setup.min.js.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_15();
		if (@sha1_file('setup/setup.min.js.php') !== '451dd1d330eafccd631e27b18ed4667ce3f9be77') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): setup/setup.min.js.php');
		}
	}
}

	warn('File could not be deleted: setup/setup_bg.png');
